Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if there is moisture in the proper towel, then it is the reons of an aposteme with a part of the uve, and for this reason one thinks that it is another uve;
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	and if moisture is between the skin of the testicles and the white muscle, then he feels warm.
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	So that when you know the color of the moisture, try on all the lower part of it, since its shape is as follows.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to this, and what comes after the insertive quarter, judge of what is within.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we treat them with fire, so that the patient becomes well according to his power and the replenishment of his body;
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	then make him lie on his back on something a little high, and put over him many blankets;
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	then make him sit on his left side, and instruct the assistant that he sits on his right side, and extend the stick to one of the two ribs at the bottom of the testicles;
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	then take the spatula, and peel off the skin of the testicles among the long hair down to its root, and make your cut completely straight while removing the skin of the testicles little by little, according to his power;
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	Then pierce the hole of water at a great height and drain all the water, and then put your fingers in it, and lift up the water.
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	and do not touch the curve of the finger, but let the water fall alone.
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	Take it all or piece by piece separately from him subtly, so that if you do not take it well washed, the water will come back.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	And if the egg was stolen from your work, if you put it back in its place when you have finished the work of the water;
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then join the two fingers of the hand together at a joint, and bandage it up as you would do with other wounds until it is well.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	And if you find the egg corrupted by some disease, then it is necessary that you hang the vessels that are suspended, in doubt of the decay of blood.
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	And then take hold of the coccyx with all the suspender, and extract the uvula, and clean it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	And if it is assembled in two parts together, knowing that these are its branches;
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	if you do the other part likewise as you did the first one, then wash the blood away, and put in the wound another wet thing made of oil;
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and put away another woolen cloth wet in wine and oil, and put it on both coccyxes, and cover with doubled sheets, and tie it all together according to this form:
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	Then take two sheets, and fill them with wool according to this form and join them together by stitching in the throat of the breeches, and one of the heads should rest on the foundation up to the back, and the other at the part of the hand;
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	and the other two on the two arms, and all is gathered up in the loop of the breastplate;
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	and never is medicine this fire cautery in place of iron size, and it is that you squeeze the cautery with a sharp tool, and scrape the skin of the feet, and is heated as we said, so that the white plague that contains the water is uncovered;
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	if you take the cautery according to this form, and pierce it with a sharp tool, and burn it with this fine cautery:
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	and coat it in all ways that you can, until you scrub everything;
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	and keep the fire from touching the egg;
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	and knows that this work is more safe;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	and maintains the prevention of blood loss, and keeps the work of ironing;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	and if there is nothing that contradicts it, or an abscess of blood or another thing, then treat what contradicts you, according to what the one who is in front says.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	And if the patient is afraid and does not want to wait for this work because of its horror, then provide a perforation, as I told you, and it is that when you are certain by the signs that we have said that the ramose water is there, then place the patient on a raised seat;
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	then pierce the abscess in the part of the back to all the broad spine, and put the perforation from long the neck;
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	and make the opening wide so that all the water runs out quickly;
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	then put cotton in the place, and bandage it, and leave to run the remaining water, then treat as the wound is healed;
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	and if the white cloth does not allow the water to come out of the wound's mouth, it is necessary that you put there a feather or the instrument with which one treats the water of the dropsical, from which the form is as described above;
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	and open the wound wide, and know that the water returns, and is gathered after six months or so, and when it is gathered as before, and in this way the patient will get better day by day.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that in the section of this essay there are many different arrangements, so it seems to me that it is better to leave it.
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	and I will tell you the work and appearances of an abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	I say then that many abscesses come from the belly, and most often from the bowels;
et c’est par mout de cas.	and it is by chance.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	This is known by bitter and water that is spread into the bowels, or from impact;
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	and the color of the abscess according to the color of the bone;
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	and do not prick at the pain, and the abscess is painful;
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	and perhaps an abscess is painful and piercing, and of pus, and never comes out of a vein, or swells up from a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is out of a vein, if it is hot by the position of the abscess, when you press it with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	and it does not suffice that you touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	What is done by swelling up from a vein is known by its position in relation to the touch with the fingers, and one can do well in making the incision on this appearance, and on the other characters;
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	and that you take care of the tips of the fingers, then the pain is in the top, and the tremor of the white part is clear, and deliver the suspension from all sides of the finger;
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the egg is already well cooked with these new charred pieces, then it is necessary that you take the egg and break it.
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	And if it is caught in the sieve, or in any of the vessels that are inside, then it is necessary that you release all those that are held, and break them up well.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	If the dislocation is at the back of the shoulder, you must reset the entire joint and remove the cause, as we have already described.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your wounds are healed, then bandage the wound with wet wool in oil and wine, and then treat it with other treatments until it is healthy.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	This is an abscess surrounded by a covering that looks like a bug, with the softening of the tissues, and the patient groans painfully when it moves.
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	And the treatment for this disease is very similar to what we have mentioned above, and we will tell you everything about the work of it, according to what the old one did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	It is necessary that you make the patient sit on a soft seat, and then pour the water from the tissues down his throat with both hands, all the way to the vessel that is closest to the penis, and wash it well, and spread it out smoothly.
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	And cut with the spetum, a sharp instrument, through the thick part of the veins, until they are completely exposed, and then peel off each piece, as we have said in the extraction of the arteries that are in the temples.
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	And then put an awl with two threads and tie it to the first loop where the vein has come together, and quickly tie it to the other end.
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	Then cut them in the middle correctly, according to the length of the body, and remove the corrupted moisture.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	Then treat the wound as you would with abow, so that no vessel bleeds from one of its ends;
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	For by this nothing comes, and all the vessels come together, so that you can pull the ends of all the vessels;
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	so that the blood does not run out from the incision of the vessels and dry up and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the syphyl
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The symptoms of this disease are either due to the sectioin that occurs or the extension on the belly in the part of the kidneys, because the intestines descend from that wound into one of the caissons.
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	and this cut is either due to the sectioin or the extension of it, and these two ways come from similar causes:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	or from impact, or from jumping, or from yelling, or from pain caused by something raised, and similar things;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	and the signs when it is due to the extension from the cut, if it is little and little, slowly and slowly, and does not suddenly come;
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	and the abscess is even until nearly at its top, so that the cut does not press on the intestine.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are when it is due to a cut of the syphyl, that sudden pain appears, and the appendages appear different, as if they were going out of the skin, and this is due to the exit of the intestines and the body away from the syphyl.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And never let the intestines twist around the colon; otherwise it will be held back and cause great pain to the patient, especially when pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	In these treatments of iron to remove fear, so that it must be avoided.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the manner of the opening so that you command the patient to keep the intestine in his hand inside the wound, if he can withdraw it;
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	And then put yourself on his neck between your hands, and loosen the ties.
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	Then take off the coat from above, and cut off all the skin of the back longwise.
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	Then place it face down on the table and cut open the skin from the waist down according to what you need to open the wound, and be careful not to hurt him.
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	Then peel off the skin from the back, making sure that the raw flesh is completely exposed and dry on all sides;
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	Then place your index finger in the space between the skin and the raw flesh that is exposed from the back, between the white skin that has come off the skin of the back, and between the second skin, and from behind the spine, and between the second skin;
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	and as you move your right hand inside the coat between your shoulders, take the white skin that has come off the back and put it on your left hand, and loosen the spine all around the wound;
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	and command to the minister that he extend the feather upward, and undo what is behind the ligature;
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and examine your two sides if there is any wrapped or white fecal matter, and if you do not find anything, pour it into the abdomen;
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	then take an needle or has a thick thread made of X threads, and pour it into the behind part of the fecal matter, which is after the skin of the anus;
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	after the cut, then cut the threads that appear from the feces, until there are four threads;
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	then assemble them one above the other in a cross shape, and tie the fecal matter, which we have said is after the skin of the anus, with a strong knot on two sides;
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	then wrap the threads around the feces and tie them together in two places so that no part of the anus can enter, and let the abscess not come out;
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and then very strictly the string according to the first string long II is of that, and after these II strings leave a syfac who is desoz the cure of the côins the great of a day;
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and then all the others according to the rondesce that the euf carries;
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	and then cut in the part which is desoz the leather of the côins, until it is no longer deformed, and let it bow, as we have said before;
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	and then bring wet wool in oil, and put it on the wounds, and let the string that we have said.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And never is cauterized the white blood that we have said, after the incision, for doubt of decay of blood.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this often happens, and leaves the string as long as it does not stick to itself;
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	and if it delays in the cheoir, so be raised by a hot water, and put on that we have said, as long as it does not stick;
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	Then heal the wound with other remedies until it is completely healed.
de hernie carnouse	of hernia carnous
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this recipe I have never seen anyone dare to make the cure with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the old one said that it is done so as the vine which is bound together, in such a way that you tie the vials, after cutting on the thigh lightly on the sole;
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	then cut it off, and heal the abscess of him who has operated, until the vials bleed;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and heal it as we have said, until it is completely healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	No time comes when there is a rupture in the arteries, as we have said, and open the veins;
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	and do not let any of the bowels come out as pieces, and if they do, it is little, and repair every hour;
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	and in any case if it stays too long in this place, if the wound or gangrene believes, until the bowels come out;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	and if there is extension of the wound that is in the angles, as we have said, for it is extended, then it is softened and swollen and opened its places;
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	and the healing process if it is by cauterization, as we have mentioned before;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and never is healed in this way:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	and he lies down on his back between your hands, then cut the place of the wound with a broad blade according to the quantity of three;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	and then remove the skin that is under the tissue that has come off, and then take a thread and tie it on the place that appears of the wound;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	and then he presses well the belly, then sews the two places that appear of the wound on the top of the thread, and sews both;
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	and then remove the thread, and do not cover the wound nor extend the ulcer nor any other thing, as I have told you in the healing of the intestine;
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	and treat with cure for wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you sew the wounds, if the wound is cured, do so until it has healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The wound-healer is necessary, and has no appearance in the laceration, and the fire-cauterization is damped at this place, and closer to salvation.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the leather of the cod
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	Many times the skin of the testicles is softened in some men, because the balls that are inside are softened, and can be seen.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	And it is necessary, when one curates him, that one make circumcision of the male member with a knife, and cut off the skin that is softened on the natural skin;
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	Then join the two lips with one stitch, and cut off the surplus of the softened skin at three stitches or four firmly;
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Then sew between the stitches, and treat it like the other wounds, until it is healed, and cut off the thread.
dou chastrement	Dou chastrement
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that chastisements are not included in our law, and for this reason I do not want to speak about them in this book;
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and it is necessary only for two ways:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	that one is that the mirrour in his sickness answereth when it is asked of him, and in his cure.
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	and the other, for since we have often had to chastise some beasts to help us, as goats and sheep and hogs and others.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say therefore that chastising is done in two ways:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	either by pulling either by cutting
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In that which we do with attraction, let us sit the beast in hot water, until the coccyx is softened and still;
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	then with your hand press them, until they are set and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	Of the chastising of the tail:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	it is necessary that you take the beast, and press the skin of the tails to your left hand, then tie the suspension, and pull on each eye with a hook when you have well scorch them;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and I leave no little pot of medicine and subtle medicine that is over the vessels;
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	and this method of cauterizing is milder than that which is done by attraction, for in attraction something may stick to the wound, so that the best lust is satisfied;
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then heal the wound as long as it is healthy.
des hermofrodites	of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermaphrodite is according to two ways as men:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	one is that between the two joints open like a woman's figure, so that it has hair, and sometimes in cort the urine.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And another way is in women, and on the head of the penis also as a penis and two testicles.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the cure for man and woman is that you rub the joints together, and cure them as other wounds;
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	in the second way, of men whose urine jumps out through the skin of the joints, there is no cure.
de la tentigene	of the tenticle
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	Tentigo is a joint that sticks to the natural part, as long as it is too ugly to see;
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	And some women have used it great as a hand, and this is the remedy.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	It is necessary that you take the surplus of the toxin from your hand or fingers, and wipe it lightly with a cotton swab.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do not cut too deep, that the blood does not run much, then heal with another cure as long as it is healthy;
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	and at another time that is born in the mouth of a cow, and employs it, and perhaps it is bad, and it is according to the appearance of a cow's disease, and for this they called him the old "cow disease".
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	If you must cut it, as we have said with the toxin, and heal it until it is well.
de erratique	de erratique
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	Erratic is when the nature of the woman has not yet been discovered, or the hernia is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and it is natural by birth, or happens by disease that comes;
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	or is it through a foreign body, or subtle poison or spice, and is made perfect in the womb, or in the coast, or in the breast, or wherever;
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and to understand conception, and childbirth, and perhaps flowers to have;
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	and the understanding of this is by the aspect of the face.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If it is close to appearing, if you want to know with your two hands or your right.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is soft and subtle medicine, and it is near to the liver, if you hurry and put it in there quickly:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	put your two fingers together, and the woman is on her back, spreading her legs;
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	then are the two kidneys formed, until the soft subtle medicine runs, and covers the stench;
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	then take wool, and soak it in oil, and put it on the place, and let the woman lie with everyone every day, so that he cannot stand.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the remedy is tough and thick, then you should chop the plant-like spaulding with a scythe.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the stench is from a horse, then hang it by the neck and cover it;
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	and have the medicines that stop the stench, as in this case, of dragon's blood, incense, together with a lot of oil;
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	then provide a broad blade, so that the wound cannot close;
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	and let it remain for a long time, and provide a dry cloth;
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat with other remedies until he is well.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when the mare becomes pregnant, if it is covered in this way, then an abscess will not form.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For if an abscess forms on the mare, one must not touch fire.
des emorroides	hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Emorrhoids are openings of veins for which without surgical operation, and when the hemorrhoids are old they become tender;
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	and we have said in the division the signs of heat, and the symptoms, and I will say here those which respond to cure.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and the thigh, when they are fully grown in the marrow, and do not appear to the touch unless it be by iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those who are at the mouth of the marrow can be felt, they are those that can be cured.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	It is therefore necessary that you put the woman in a cold house, then bind the tender parts to the scales, and cut off at the roots, then powder on medicines that restrain blood, as if it were due to heat and dragon's blood and similar things;
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	then pour water on its feet against the wall for an hour, then put it in cold water;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	and if the fever comes, then let the medicine be made with a decoction of sumac and pomegranate rinds and gall and similar things, and then take barley flour, and confect it with honey and so forth, and make an ointment out of it to put on his back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it stops, that's good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	Or if not, then let him have hot towels on his back and not hurt the skin;
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	then take another, and moisten it with juice of plantain or of oak apple, and apply it to the sore spot.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess has healed, then let him stop applying ointment once he is well.
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	And that which is called "balathyr" is red, and looks like a sharp lance, then cover it as I have said before.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat him until he is well.
des apostemes de la marris	The abscesses of the breast
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Various types of abscess can occur in the breast, such as syphilis, piercing abscess, herpes, écoulement, fistules, hemorrhoids, hot abscess, and many other diseases I have mentioned in the division.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	It is necessary that I say in this treatise about the abscess that comes in the breast, which is not an abscess that hurts only;
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	and if you can see the heat of iron, if you look at the abscess when it is beginning to come, and full of heat and fever, and if it becomes red, then you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Then do not hurry to pierce it, but let it die while the pain is relieved;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	and then put the patient on a bed, and have two small chairs where he leans his legs, and support his feet in different directions from the leg;
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	and let their hips be spread apart, and put their arms out on their knees, and bind them well with a good rope;
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	then suck the bite toward the right side of the mouth, and I bring the instrument with which one operates the mouth of the breast, so that afterwards it comes into form;
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	and it is necessary that when you see this instrument used, that you place the ring first in order to know the depth of the wound, so that what enters into the instrument does not come out imperfectly and does not wound the patient.
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	and if the instrument is larger, it is necessary to cover the depth of the wound with cloth, so that the instrument does not harm the patient.
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	and it is necessary that he put the tip of the instrument above, and that he darken the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	And when the abscess opens, and you hold it with your hand, if it is necessary to cover the tip, at the spittle's base;
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	and when the bowels are empty, if you put wet cloths in the wound soaked in rose oil or dry green oil;
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	and dip the tent of the wound in the marsh all the way to the bottom, and dip the other end on the top of the hand above the knuckle, wet with water or cooked wool.
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then the healer after two days of poultice coming to this, as long as it is well;
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and no more raise the marsh and the wound by a hot water and honey poultice, and then water or roots of flowers and arnica are cooked.
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	then recover to the poultice.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound has closed over the bone, you must not cook it with iron, but treat it as we have said in the chapter on wounds.
de l’enfantement	of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	Artisan is first at the birth that it knows the shape of natural birth, and the signs if you see the woman rushing down, and desires to smell the air.
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	then the child rushes to come out;
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	then you know that these births are according to the natural shape, and the first one comes out with his head, and the second with him;
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	and when you see these signs, if it is convenient to press lightly his belly, so that the baby comes soon;
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	For when he defecates on top of his head, if the second one is with him, and is washed out by good purification;
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	and what comes otherwise does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For it never comes on its feet, and comes from the neck or shoulders, and the hands, or sometimes on his belly, or often, and is transformed by accident on his throat, and by other bad shapes;
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	So it is necessary for the dance to be wise and subtle in these things, and to beware of error and deception, and I will show you all the shapes how to help him.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the baby comes on top of his head by natural birth, and the woman gives birth to grief, and his virtue is weak, then the fair one sits on a saddle, or the women hold her;
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	and then made of it an oil or fenugreek is boiled, and then poured between the two small spatumiles which are here the form:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	and then split the second one, and cover with his nail until the moisture that is inside comes out.
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	and press on the woman's belly until the baby comes out, and if it does not come out, then it is necessary to use a muscle- relaxing paste of fenugreek oil with sise-seed oil;
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	then make her lie down and cough, and keep her mouth and nose covered for an hour:
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	now let the baby come out.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if the two hands come out hard, then you must gently twist them back and forth;
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot go in, then put the woman on a chair and raise her feet;
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	and then at the top of the seat on the ground, and paint on the woman, so that she does not fall while standing;
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	and his hands cannot enter, and the baby dies if he holds his hands on the knife that is placed in front, and pulls out the child, and leaves it even.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	from delivery of the child between his feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child comes on its feet, so let him come up;
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then turn it little by little until it is even;
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then stretch it little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	Until it jumps just as high as the knuckles, so she is ordered to bend down, and makes her shake with fear;
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	If you jump, then God help you.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if he does not jump as we have said, then turn him little by little so that he is according to the natural shape.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then he is light-headed.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it does not come as we have said, then take muscle from the back, and oil of sisle, and gum melted, and grind all in a mortar;
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and sit on the nature of the woman inside and away this ointment, then let her sit in water until she is soaked the ribs;
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when it is wet soaked, then let him do a chain of myrrh, and put it off, and let it lie for an hour;
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then let her sit on a seat, then make her sneeze and straiten her mouth and nose, and pinch her belly lightly, for the fetuses jump now.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	of the delivery of the child between her legs
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	and when the fetus comes in this form, if I put the belly his hands poking and poking;
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	then let it be ligated on its neck, and let the feet hang down, and let it lie on its back;

et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	and if he falls, so don't take your feet and move your body, then move your stomach up, then pour your hands.
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	and the child pokes and pokes;
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	and order the woman to stretch herself as long as the child is.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	the delivery of the child who comes with a wide hand hanging down one side at a time
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	it comes to bring back the hand;
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	if you can't bring it back, so the woman stands up and goes;
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	if she can't go, so make her sit up on a bed, and put her feet together;
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	then arrange the muscles as I have described;
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	and if she doesn't give birth, so make her sit on a chair, and then study to bring back the hand;
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	and the child according to the natural form, and makes it shake, and orders her to stretch herself as long as the child is.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	The child's delivery from his mother's womb, and he spread his hands wide, and turned his face toward her back.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It is fitting that the surgeon clean his hands, then wash them little by little, and dry them lightly.
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	And when he is clean, if he puts on the muslin bandage of cotton and oil as we have said, then he commands that she moves little by little;
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	And when you have done this, if the fire is placed in a position, and he commands that it be heated;
et la fai esternuer.	and then he makes it shake.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	of this same manner to all the second time
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When he comes in this way for all the second time, if you cut off his fingernail, as long as the moisture is empty;
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if he hangs himself by the neck, so that it cuts off his breath, so that he does not hold back, and the hangman dies;
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	Then pour the child in, as long as you have put it in the right way, and command the woman that she does not shake herself at all:
adonques si istra legierement.	So then if lightly.
de l’issue des gemelz	of twins
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	For it is known that many are born, and only three or four at a time.
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	and this is not an extraordinary thing, and seldom happens.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	Two are an extraordinary thing, and rarely live, if one does not know.
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that, which are multiplied, and are desired by the doctor who devises them, who is tied to the bodge;
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	and they are not born naturally as all of us do, if we have said it.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they are born lightly, as we have said, and the subtle doctor, and quickly and lightly does what he does;
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	and make it so that it is worth doing for salvation.
de plusors enfans	of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	And they are not formed in the womb of one or two or three or four or five or six or seven, or more than fifteen until they are shaped like a child by the measure of the wise glory, and the doctor knows all this, for perhaps similar things happen to him;
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	Make it according to what is necessary.
de l’enfant mort	of the dead child
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat a woman with a dead fetus or an aborted child, as I said in the division, and it does not come out, and you are forced to use your hands;
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	if it is appropriate that you know whether the woman is of sound health, and she has no accident or fear of death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	if it is appropriate that the woman be seated on her heels, with her knees bent toward her chest and her legs raised;
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	and the assistant applies the poultice to both parts, so that she is laid on a bed as if she were about to give birth to a child;
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	Then rub the mouth of the pregnant woman with wet oil made from amaranth and fenugrec and linseed seed, then anoint her hands with these oils and these musk ambrosia;
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	Then place the bottle lightly in the sea, and then take care that he who drinks does not drink too much wine that is suitable for him, and be careful that the one who drinks does not get dressed up so that he comes to his head.
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	if he puts the wine in his hair or in his throat or in his mouth or in his palate or cuts it with a razor or near the sides, and if he drinks, he will be drunk on his feet, he will fall down or he will cut himself at the edges;
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and it is convenient that he hold the bottle in his right hand, and place the cup between his two hands with his left hand, and pour the wine lightly in all of these places until it comes to the empty thing;
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	this is the form of the wine;
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then put another bottle together, so that the extraction is even;
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then stand it equally by moving it from one side to the other, so that it can be set, and hold the lower teeth together with a bit of force, like this:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	If one part stops moving, if you rub some oil on its two sides and press it in that part, and then pull the other part;
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if one part doesn't move at all, place this tooth higher up or lower down, and do so until it has set completely.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes before the other and cannot return due to a spasm, you must wrap it in a sheet so that it sets completely.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	Then cut into the joint of the foot or at the neck, and in the other hand also, and between the toes.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the child's hip is large and it is stuck in the birth canal, or if there is an acute angle, you must push the thorny spatula between your two hips, and push the angle and extract the spike.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	where you hold the instrument which is called "almond", from which the form comes with the instruments or chalk that follows this one;
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	and so I make it fix itself by nature;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	and then draw out the bones with pliers, and the head of the shoulder is torn out with force if it does not come off easily, until the moisture that is there comes out;
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	and if it cannot come out, then break it into pieces with a hammer so you can remove it;
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	and if it is swollen in the belly or under the ribs, so that it is necessary to pierce you until the moisture runs;
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if he falls on his feet, if it is a light atraction, and if we bring him to the mouth of the mare, it is easy.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is dislocated in the belly or in the hip, so that you must take off the bandages wrapped around the hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and break the belly or hip, until the moisture that is there runs;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if his other member is osteitic, and the head remains, then he pulls his hand away completely from the marrow, and draws it up to the mouth of the marrow;
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then I pour some wine or two, and draw it out strongly;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the mouth of the marrow is constricted by heat that has come to it, so that it cannot work any more, then one must provide moist and greasy things;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and he provides with plasters, and cuts in acidic, moistening, and softening things.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the wound is on his ribcage, and you can make it even, then provide what we have said for a live child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	and if one does not have the power, then he draws it out in pieces, and leaves nothing of the second one.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And when you have done this, provide what we have said for warm, new marrow that comes from the marrow;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if blood flow occurs, then if it is put in water it is restrained, and other treatments are given.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whose womb a child had been killed, then consult another on that one, and it was killed again.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time the wound began to swell and then it broke open and there was a great pus.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to treat it, and I thought for a long time, but I couldn't close the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I put on a plaster of strong attraction, and there put an arm, and after a few days another.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I marvelled much, for this man's belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought it was the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I want to bandage the wound, and hold them together as long as the woman was in a better state;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	and wait for the woman to be longer than ten years, and it was fixed a little bow from its place;
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	and I have remembered this medicine only that when the master tries an strange thing, he may know how to put help.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	to bring the married woman back to her place
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Here comes the form of the pressure, where we pull the books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	and at two turns are two shoulders.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	However, the horns are more subtle than the restraint, and it is made of oak or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	and the mouth of the horn must be very wide, and the margins of the trees must be, and a length of about one palm and a half;
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and the two limbs be twice the length of this half palm, or a little longer.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and these two joints are inserted into the mouth of the socket to open when the two horns are turned.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, its appearance more subtle and lighter, is made of oak or boxwood, according to the shape of the claws;
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and have two joints, as you see, a palm long and two fingers wide;
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you see the socket opened for all the instrument, so that the woman sits on the bed, her legs hanging down and her feet spread out, then set the two joints together in the socket, and hold the top of the instrument between her knees;
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	then open your hand for all the instrument, just as you did for the claws evenly, according to the quantity that you see the mouth of the socket opened, until the ball makes what she wants;
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	All these instruments are completely assembled, and they are multiplied by their appearances.
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	And when you have prepared the instruments, then the operation is faster, and higher up for its quantity.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	Do not despair about the instrument unless you have prepared it, for its necessity is not excusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the second is retained for childbirth, it is necessary that you command the disease to keep its hair, and then she makes her stand and shake from condition, and her hands are drawn back to the mouth and neck;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	and if it does not hold, well is it.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, if I can take it, and make a hole or cover, and put herbs that can open the mouth of the sick, as calamus, rue, anise, chamomile, cassia and centaury;
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	all these herbs, or none of them, are cooked or boiled in water on the fire;
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	and then place a tube or hole at the tip of the pot, and the other end in the mouth of the wound, and suck out the vapors that come into the wound;
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	then make her sneeze, as we have said.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If you do not let him get well soon.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	If she remains well after this treatment and is not better, order her to soak her left hand in oil of saffron or in a muscadine mixture of alto, and then pour it out again, and do it a second time;
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and when she has found it, if she pricks it and stretches it little by little correctly, so that the wound does not break at the extraction;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but make her move it lightly from side to side, and then draw it out;
si venra et se desaerdra.	then it will come out and fall away.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the mouth of the wound is tight and constricted, we have said the treatment of sneezing, and of vaporizing herbs;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if it is not of all those we have said, so guard that you do not follow the treatment.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but it is necessary that he who is in the mouth of the mare, you tie him to the cunt of the woman, then you cauterize with ointment tetrafarmer.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	if she gets worse and comes again, it will be fierce;
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	but first, when the wound is infected with a bad smell in the stomach and head of the patient, and blisters on the disease.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	So it is necessary to smoke in an appropriate way:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	neither of the old have experienced smoking with watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The shape of the instrument by which one smokes the woman to retain the flowers and the second is such:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	and it is as if to a dog, and put the head gently in the smoke, and the shoulders wide over the fire;
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	and let the smoke be on the coals, and burn it until it is spent, and begin another.
de percier lou fondement	to pierce through the foundation
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born who have not yet had their foundations pierced, but they are cut off by a subtle surgeon.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	If it is necessary that he who cuts with the surgeon pierce his foundation at his own will, and does not cut with a small chisel and seal the seam so that he does not touch it;
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	then dip in another moisture with wine and oil, then treat with ointment until it is well.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will not return, then place or pierce a hole with an awl, and let the hand remain extended, and be careful when he goes to bed.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And never comes a sudden cauterization of a wound or an abscess;
si covient coper celui soudement:	If it is necessary to cover the sudden cauterization:
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	if sooth, if as we have said of the wine of plunging.
de la fistule dou fondement	of the fistula of the fundament
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistulas which come from the foundation are an expansion, and more difficult to come than from the foundation of the members, or in the space between the two parts, if it is one or more fistulas;
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	and when this foundation is old, if you open it, and a little dampness comes out white or subtle bow, and these fistulas are never persisting;
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	and are caused by what is in this area of excretion or ventosity when the patient does excretion, and perhaps in leap some towards.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And if fistulas that pierce just up to the bladder, and just up to the half of the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and arrive just up to the junction of the thigh, and just up to the notch of the neck.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And so one knows that the persistent fistula is at the foundation, and does not persist:
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and is that you pierce your second finger or foundation, and pierce a small needle of silver or iron in the fistula when there is no twists:
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	and if there is twists, if you pierce with a small string of rope or a horse's hair, as long as you feel the string or hair in your finger:
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and does not come from perforation of vomiting or wind, nor see as we have said:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	that it does not pierce at all.
si te haste dou curer.	if you hurry to heal.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula reaches the bladder or the conduit of urine, if it causes urine to flow, and cannot be controlled by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is pierced only up to the join of the crotch, if is the tent that comes up to the place.
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is no twist and the invention of the pain inside, if it is that he comes soon, and does not come medicine nor suddenly by rubbing;
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	and in these persisting abscesses there is no cure except work, and vanity of foolish dreams that enter into them.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In the one that is not persistent and not old, there is hope of health by fire, as I have experienced, and it is that the patient lies between your hands on his back;
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	and let his legs hang down to his knees, and let his knees bend towards his belly;
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then pour water into a tub, or mud if there is a twist, until you know where the tub comes from.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels pain in his back, then pour water on your two fingers, and it will feel like the tub has pierced him;
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	and is uncovered where you feel between your thumb and the finger next to it, then know that it is a persistent wound;
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	if it does not hurt, then it cannot be cured.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	One should try all means to cure some, but most of them do not work;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	and the help that can be given, if one heats the fine cauldron according to the width of the fistula, as it is said above;
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	and put all the heat into the tube, until it comes out smoothly from the base;
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	and make it twice or three times, as long as you know that these charred things are like an owl's feather;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	and then the doctor of wet tenders bathes it, until that char comes out, and then the doctor of ointment makes a char and binds it up.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If it is done thus, it is good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this, otherwise it cannot be healed;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	and if it is tried between, and does not pierce until the top which is at the base, and on either side of the tube there is a thick covering of char or of medicine, and you see the tube at the place where the covering begins to move;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	if the cover of the tube of the fistula is cut off and reset before the tube, and then the fire is applied after it, until it comes to the top of the tube;
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	and will be delivered the test, and shall be strong;
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	then my god shall deliver those charred trees that seem like a feather of an owl, and none remain thereat.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if you have a fever, and heat comes between you and the work, then fire cautery or an acrid medicine.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery brings together two things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	that is to say, on the one hand, the burning of these charred shoulders, and on the other, the evacuation of blood and drying up of moisture.
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	then the healer of wet tents will dry or roast it, until its leathery layer is peeled off, and those charred shoulders are roasted in the fire;
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	then heal the wound of the rusting hard shoulders, and these dry remedies are applied.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is reset, if it is well and does not return to its place.
