et puis lie lou lien qui est parmi les asseles au tornet devers le chief, et l’autre liien devers les piez a l’autre tornet, et chescuns des ministres torne son tornet a tout le liien, et li maistres mette l’espinee igal si com nos avons dit.	and then let the line be laid that is among the torches to the twist opposite the head, and the other line toward the torches, and each minister twist his own line, and the master put the pegs at equal intervals as we have said.
Et quant elle est igalz, si met sus emplaustre desiccatif avec abun d’uef, et puis les estoupes, et puis l’estele d’une tablete de III dois de lonc, que porpreigne lou leu de la gilbositeit et la partie de l’espondile sainne, puis le lie d’un liien, si com nos avons dit, et use li malaides de norrissement subtil, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when it is even, put on dried plaster with much honey, and then the patches, and then the wood from a tablet of three inches long, which turns red when it comes into contact with the gangrene and the part of the spine that is healthy, and tie it with a thread, as we have said, and use subtle fasting for the patient until he is well.
et s’aucune chose vient en la fin de la santez, si covient aministrer medicines amollissans et asouajans, avec l’estele que nos avons dit ci devant;	and if nothing comes in the end of the health, then administer softening and soothing medicines with the wood that we have said above.
et aucune fois i aministre on une piece de plonc, et aucune fois vient li apparance en la derriere spondile dou dos, et cuide on que ce soit dislocations;	and never give a piece of plaster, and never does the appearance come in the lower spine at the back, and be careful that it is not dislocations;
et c’est li os qui apert, por coi on n’i doit mie avoir presumption:	This is the bone that opens, for one should not have any presumption:
par aventure feroit venir la mort.	for fear that death might come.
des dislocations de la hainche	dislocations of the hip joint
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures;	It is known that the hips and shoulder joints only come from dislocations, not at all like the other joints.
et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc IIII parties:	and the hip joint is dislocated according to four parts:
dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier;	behind and in front;
et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	and more behind them, and less dislocated in front and behind.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	And the knowledge of its dislocations behind is that when one joins the sick leg with the healthy one, it is farther away, and the sick knees are higher than the healthy ones, and the sick man cannot double his knee in fire;
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	and the legs that are swollen with heat from an abscess, so that the head of the thigh comes out.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	And the sign of that which comes outside is that this accident is opposite to those before.
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;	And the signs of him who is in front are that his leg is straight according to the fittingness;
toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	all the way, don't double up on the knee pain, and if you let it walk, you can't do it before, and hold back your urine, and swell the ankle, and when you go, you go over the heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the signs of him who has been behind, if he cannot spread his knee, nor double it, and is this leg more twisted than the other, and the ankle is softened, and the hipbone is in its place among the ribs.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	Those who come to this dislocation appearance should know that if the dislocation is old, and it delays according to its disposition, there is no treatment;
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	and it doesn't make sense for him to have presumptuousness.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;	And in those who have a fresh dislocation, and there are four ways of dislocation, if you hurry to restore the joint, and turn it inside out and outside in, and move it to the right and left;
par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	So that it may return, and there is no need for any other treatment;
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	If it doesn't return in this way, you must prepare a strong minister, and hold the leg very strongly with both hands, or tie it where it is tied to the knee;
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	and other ministers extend their hand above in a certain way that he bottle his hands of his asses, then he strangles with a string on the cunt;
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	and other tings take the hair from the loins;
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	and extend upwards and downwards all at once, so that the patient is raised up from the ground all at once, and remains there.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as IIII semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	And this way of extension is common to four resemblances, and if the dislocation has returned, as we have said, it is good.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	If not, then one should put a cure to his appearance.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	When the dislocations are in the back, you must lie the patient on his back, then put the string on the root of the cunt, and the line that is out of its place, then extend the line upwards towards the anus, and downwards towards the root.
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	Then other ministers take his arms, and embrace the big line of the cunt of the patient, and extend it to both sides in a certain form:
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	If he returns to his place now;
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	and this method of dislocation is lighter than others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	And if you cannot hold it in this way that we have described, then it is necessary that you tie the two feet of the patient together with a strong rope from the heel, and on the thigh, and extend the sore leg twice as far as the other;
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	then hang it by the neck of a post, and be hung from the ground two long arms;
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	and order one minister to embrace the head of the patient, and have other ministers hang with him who embrace the hips in a way that the joints return quickly;
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation is away, so the patient lies down as we have described in the one who has giddy-head, and remove the rope from the leg properly, and also on the waist;
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	then put two sticks, one at the head and another at the feet, then stick a stick between the legs of the sick person so that it fits into the form;
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	and let hang damp towels inside, so that it does not burn the sick person, then extend each minister towards him, and let him put the dislocation in his hand at an equal distance from his body.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns, it is good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If not, set on .ie. a table, and press it thus as we said in the gibosity, and lay the patient on the sound side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when the dislocations are in front, if it is necessary to extend the sick leg quickly, and according to what I have said;
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	and let him put his pain on the sick leg, then press with the other hand, and extend it towards the knee;
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if the dislocations are at the back, if it is not necessary to extend the sick person backwards, do not lift him up from the ground, but rather let him fall backwards as he was lying; so that he falls on his two hind legs, as we have said when lying down on the two legs;
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	and over his face, and the leg extended as we have said above, and must all be pressed together on the joint at the table;
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	and will be at a point when the patient extends his legs, and they shall be even;
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	then fix the knees, and put on the plaster, and extract a bandage, so that the ankle does not move;
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	and rest for three or four days, then remove it, and put on the plaster;
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	and if you see that they are even, then extract it, as before, and leave it for three days;
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	then remove it, and let him walk loudly, until the limbs are comfortable.
de la dislocation dou genoil	from the dislocation of the hip joint
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The genius is dislocated according to three manners:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	that is to say, inside and outside, and behind.
et ne desalue point devant.	and do not dislocate in front.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the signs are that you instruct the patient that he bend his leg to his crotch, and if it does not bend to his crotch, know that it is dislocated.
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	and the reduction of all is that you make the patient sit upright, and extend his leg if he can, and place your back on his face, and place his foot on your feet;
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	then take his knee between your palms, and draw back between your two, then bend the two ribs of the knee together;
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	and other ministers extend his foot, until the genoux returns to its place, and the signs are that he bends his leg to his crotch lightly;
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	and put the plaster on, and make the leg bend at the crotch, and keep it together firmly for three or four days, then remove it;
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	and do not work on the patient's pain, as long as the limbs are comfortable.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the members are not at their place, if one administer a strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of the hip, until they are healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	of the dislocation from the heel
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are never dislocated, nor completely displaced inward or outward.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	and the signs are that the ankle is dislocated, and try before the part where it has been displaced:
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	let them stretch lightly if they are light, and they must extend lightly with their hands when they are slightly bruised.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And if it is displaced from the top, you must make the patient sit upright, and tie him down except for the leg, above the ankle;
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	then train the foot with your right hand, and then with your left hand twice, and then raise it up, and blow on the foot well up;
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	and do this twice, as we have said, blowing and training the foot;
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	if it comes back, it is good;
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	if not, then begin again, because it returns;
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	and if it cannot come back in this way, then take the sick person on their back on the ground, and place a hard pass firmly in the ground between their legs, and tie the drapes around, so that he does not hurt the sick.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	then wrap the minister's hip, and another minister extends the leg to its hands or ties it, so that he lies on the neck of the stone;
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	then extend each minister equally, and the pass should be close between the sick person's hips to hold the sick person down;
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	then place the mirror of dislocation in the minister's hands, and another minister ties the healthy leg to the side, and the dislocation will come back slowly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it is set, then apply the plaster and press it down, and strain it well, and tie the foot to the leg, and guard against the joints that are on the back of the ankle, so that the ties are not too tight;
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	and leave it II days or III, and bind it loose, if he draws.
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	and release it on the third day or fourth, and protect the patient from going out for four days;
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	and if he goes before that term is up, it is not yet certain that he will not dislocate again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the abscesses come to a head, so that you calm it, as we have said elsewhere, until it is well.
des dois	the two
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the two are dislocated, so that they are nicely extended without work, and this is a light thing.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in any joint of his back or foot, then you must make the patient sit upright on a flat bed or chair, and put your foot on that which opens these joints, then press your foot firmly, until he regains feeling;
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	and when it is healed, and does not open anymore, then place the sole of his foot on a table at four corners, then press firmly, and leave it for three days, then release him;
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and let him rest, until he is well.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wound and dislocation together
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound comes with a dislocation, and it is restored, many times the patient has died:
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	If you are not presumptuous in the cure, if you are not skilled in this art and have not used it for a long time, and if you are not compassionate and merciful and slow to anger, do not be too hasty.
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	and at the beginning of things use soothing ointment on an abscess, and leave the patient in God's hands if you see no hope for health;
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	and when you see hope, now set the limb back in place so that the abscesses may come;
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	and when the limb is in place, administer soothing ointment to the wound and treat it with dry poultices as appropriate;
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	and if there has been a fracture with joint displacement and some small bones have broken, then do as we said for simple illnesses;
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	and keep yourself from going down the path of fear, according to what I have said, for it will bring you into difficulty according to your Creator, and for the sake of saving your life and your body.
